MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

[See rule 329]
Companies Act, 1956
[Members Voluntary Winding-up]
In matters of
PHOENIX KNOWLEDGE SERVICE PRIVATE LIMITED
(CIN:U72300TN2005PTC057464)
Notice Convening Final Meeting
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 that a Final Meeting of the members of the above-named
company will be held at the Registered Office of the Company Situated at “CAPITAL PLACE”, New No.16
(Old No.50), South Boag Road, T.Nagar, Chennai-600 017, on Wednesday the 26th day of April, 2017 at
11.00 A.M. for the purpose of having the accounts laid before them showing the manner in which the winding-up
has been conducted and the property of the company disposed of and of hearing any explanation that may be
given by the liquidator and also of determining by a special resolution of the company, the manner in which the
books, accounts and documents of the company and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.
Chennai,
24th March 2017.

MUTHULAKSHMI GANESH,
Liquidator.

the books, accounts and documents of the company and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.
Chennai,
24th March 2017.

R SRIDHARAN,
Liquidator.
